Traverse the music folder, collecting each subfolder's ModTime (self or any non-dir children, whichever is newer)\n69: // For each changed folder: get all files from DB whose path starts with the changed folder (non-recursively), check each file:\n70: // - if file in folder is newer, update the one in DB\n71: // - if file in folder does not exists in DB, add it\n72: // - for each file in the
